CURL_HTTP_VERSION_1_0, /* please use HTTP 1.0 in the request */\n  CURL_HTTP_VERSION_1_1, /* please use HTTP 1.1 in the request */\n  CURL_HTTP_VERSION_2_0, /* please use HTTP 2 in the request */\n
